\DoxyCodeLine{1371   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Const>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1372   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_STYLE\_FLAG\_XXX                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1373   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1374   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1375   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A list of bit-\/flags used to indicate the style of a given face.    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1376   \textcolor{comment}{/*    These are used in the `style\_flags' field of @FT\_FaceRec.          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1377   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1378   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Values>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1379   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_STYLE\_FLAG\_ITALIC ::                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1380   \textcolor{comment}{/*      Indicates that a given face style is italic or oblique.          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1381   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1382   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_STYLE\_FLAG\_BOLD ::                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1383   \textcolor{comment}{/*      Indicates that a given face is bold.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1384   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1385   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1386   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The style information as provided by FreeType is very basic.  More */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1387   \textcolor{comment}{/*    details are beyond the scope and should be done on a higher level  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1388   \textcolor{comment}{/*    (for example, by analyzing various fields of the `OS/2' table in   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1389   \textcolor{comment}{/*    SFNT based fonts).                                                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1390   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1391 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_STYLE\_FLAG\_ITALIC  ( 1 << 0 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1392 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_STYLE\_FLAG\_BOLD    ( 1 << 1 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1393 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1394 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1395 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1396   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1397   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Type>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1398   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Size\_Internal                                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1399   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1400   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1402   \textcolor{comment}{/*    model private data of a given @FT\_Size object.                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1403   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1404   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }FT\_Size\_InternalRec\_*  FT\_Size\_Internal;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1405 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1406 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1407 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1408   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1409   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Struct>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1410   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Size\_Metrics                                                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1411   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1412   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1413   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The size metrics structure gives the metrics of a size object.     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1414   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1415   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Fields>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1416   \textcolor{comment}{/*    x\_ppem       :: The width of the scaled EM square in pixels, hence */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1417   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    the term `ppem' (pixels per EM).  It is also       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1418   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    referred to as `nominal width'.                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1419   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1420   \textcolor{comment}{/*    y\_ppem       :: The height of the scaled EM square in pixels,      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1421   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    hence the term `ppem' (pixels per EM).  It is also */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1422   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    referred to as `nominal height'.                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1423   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1424   \textcolor{comment}{/*    x\_scale      :: A 16.16 fractional scaling value used to convert   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1425   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    horizontal metrics from font units to 26.6         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1426   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    fractional pixels.  Only relevant for scalable     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1427   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    font formats.                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1428   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1429   \textcolor{comment}{/*    y\_scale      :: A 16.16 fractional scaling value used to convert   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1430   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    vertical metrics from font units to 26.6           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1431   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    fractional pixels.  Only relevant for scalable     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1432   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    font formats.                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1433   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1434   \textcolor{comment}{/*    ascender     :: The ascender in 26.6 fractional pixels.  See       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1435   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    @FT\_FaceRec for the details.                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1436   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1437   \textcolor{comment}{/*    descender    :: The descender in 26.6 fractional pixels.  See      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1438   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    @FT\_FaceRec for the details.                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1439   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1440   \textcolor{comment}{/*    height       :: The height in 26.6 fractional pixels.  See         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1441   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    @FT\_FaceRec for the details.                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1442   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1443   \textcolor{comment}{/*    max\_advance  :: The maximum advance width in 26.6 fractional       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1444   \textcolor{comment}{/*                    pixels.  See @FT\_FaceRec for the details.          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1445   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1446   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1447   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The scaling values, if relevant, are determined first during a     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1448   \textcolor{comment}{/*    size changing operation.  The remaining fields are then set by the */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1449   \textcolor{comment}{/*    driver.  For scalable formats, they are usually set to scaled      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1450   \textcolor{comment}{/*    values of the corresponding fields in @FT\_FaceRec.                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1451   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1452   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Note that due to glyph hinting, these values might not be exact    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1453   \textcolor{comment}{/*    for certain fonts.  Thus they must be treated as unreliable        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1454   \textcolor{comment}{/*    with an error margin of at least one pixel!                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1455   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1456   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Indeed, the only way to get the exact metrics is to render \_all\_   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1457   \textcolor{comment}{/*    glyphs.  As this would be a definite performance hit, it is up to  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1458   \textcolor{comment}{/*    client applications to perform such computations.                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1459   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1460   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The FT\_Size\_Metrics structure is valid for bitmap fonts also.      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1461   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1462   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct  }\mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Size__Metrics__}{FT\_Size\_Metrics\_}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1463   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1464     FT\_UShort  x\_ppem;      \textcolor{comment}{/* horizontal pixels per EM               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1465     FT\_UShort  y\_ppem;      \textcolor{comment}{/* vertical pixels per EM                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1466 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1467     FT\_Fixed   x\_scale;     \textcolor{comment}{/* scaling values used to convert font    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1468     FT\_Fixed   y\_scale;     \textcolor{comment}{/* units to 26.6 fractional pixels        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1469 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1470     FT\_Pos     ascender;    \textcolor{comment}{/* ascender in 26.6 frac. pixels          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1471     FT\_Pos     descender;   \textcolor{comment}{/* descender in 26.6 frac. pixels         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1472     FT\_Pos     height;      \textcolor{comment}{/* text height in 26.6 frac. pixels       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1473     FT\_Pos     max\_advance; \textcolor{comment}{/* max horizontal advance, in 26.6 pixels */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1474 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1475   \} \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Size__Metrics__}{FT\_Size\_Metrics}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1476 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1477 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1478 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1479   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1480   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Struct>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1481   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_SizeRec                                                         */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1485   \textcolor{comment}{/*    object at a given size.                                            */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1490   \textcolor{comment}{/*    generic :: A typeless pointer, unused by the FreeType library or   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1491   \textcolor{comment}{/*               any of its drivers.  It can be used by client           */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1494   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1495   \textcolor{comment}{/*    metrics :: Metrics for this size object.  This field is read-\/only. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1496   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1497   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct  }\mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__SizeRec__}{FT\_SizeRec\_}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1507 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1508   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1509   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Struct>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1510   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_SubGlyph                                                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1511   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1512   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1513   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The subglyph structure is an internal object used to describe      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1514   \textcolor{comment}{/*    subglyphs (for example, in the case of composites).                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1515   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1516   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1517   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The subglyph implementation is not part of the high-\/level API,     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1518   \textcolor{comment}{/*    hence the forward structure declaration.                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1519   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1520   \textcolor{comment}{/*    You can however retrieve subglyph information with                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1521   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Get\_SubGlyph\_Info.                                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1522   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1523   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }FT\_SubGlyphRec\_*  FT\_SubGlyph;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1524 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1525 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1526 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1527   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1528   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Type>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1529   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Slot\_Internal                                                   */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1534   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1535   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }FT\_Slot\_InternalRec\_*  FT\_Slot\_Internal;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1536 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1537 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1538 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1539   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1540   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Struct>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1541   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_GlyphSlotRec                                                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1542   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1543   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1544   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FreeType root glyph slot class structure.  A glyph slot is a       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1545   \textcolor{comment}{/*    container where individual glyphs can be loaded, be they in        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1546   \textcolor{comment}{/*    outline or bitmap format.                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1547   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1548   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Fields>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1549   \textcolor{comment}{/*    library           :: A handle to the FreeType library instance     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1550   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         this slot belongs to.                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1551   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1552   \textcolor{comment}{/*    face              :: A handle to the parent face object.           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1553   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1554   \textcolor{comment}{/*    next              :: In some cases (like some font tools), several */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1555   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         glyph slots per face object can be a good     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1556   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         thing.  As this is rare, the glyph slots are  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1557   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         listed through a direct, single-\/linked list   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1558   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         using its `next' field.                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1559   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1560   \textcolor{comment}{/*    generic           :: A typeless pointer unused by the FreeType     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1561   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         library or any of its drivers.  It can be     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1562   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         used by client applications to link their own */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1563   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         data to each glyph slot object.               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1564   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1565   \textcolor{comment}{/*    metrics           :: The metrics of the last loaded glyph in the   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1566   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         slot.  The returned values depend on the last */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1567   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         load flags (see the @FT\_Load\_Glyph API        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1568   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         function) and can be expressed either in 26.6 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1569   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         fractional pixels or font units.              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1570   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1571   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         Note that even when the glyph image is        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1572   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         transformed, the metrics are not.             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1573   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1574   \textcolor{comment}{/*    linearHoriAdvance :: The advance width of the unhinted glyph.      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1575   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         Its value is expressed in 16.16 fractional    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1576   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         pixels, unless @FT\_LOAD\_LINEAR\_DESIGN is set  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1577   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         when loading the glyph.  This field can be    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1578   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         important to perform correct WYSIWYG layout.  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1579   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         Only relevant for outline glyphs.             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1580   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1581   \textcolor{comment}{/*    linearVertAdvance :: The advance height of the unhinted glyph.     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1582   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         Its value is expressed in 16.16 fractional    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1583   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         pixels, unless @FT\_LOAD\_LINEAR\_DESIGN is set  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1584   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         when loading the glyph.  This field can be    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1585   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         important to perform correct WYSIWYG layout.  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1586   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         Only relevant for outline glyphs.             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1587   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1588   \textcolor{comment}{/*    advance           :: This shorthand is, depending on               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1589   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         @FT\_LOAD\_IGNORE\_TRANSFORM, the transformed    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1590   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         (hinted) advance width for the glyph, in 26.6 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1591   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         fractional pixel format.  As specified with   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1592   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         @FT\_LOAD\_VERTICAL\_LAYOUT, it uses either the  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1593   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         `horiAdvance' or the `vertAdvance' value of   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1594   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         `metrics' field.                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1595   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1596   \textcolor{comment}{/*    format            :: This field indicates the format of the image  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1597   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         contained in the glyph slot.  Typically       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1598   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_BITMAP,                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1599   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_OUTLINE, or                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1600   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_COMPOSITE, but others are    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1601   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         possible.                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1602   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1603   \textcolor{comment}{/*    bitmap            :: This field is used as a bitmap descriptor     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1604   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         when the slot format is                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1605   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_BITMAP.  Note that the       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1606   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         address and content of the bitmap buffer can  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1607   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         change between calls of @FT\_Load\_Glyph and a  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1608   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         few other functions.                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1609   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1610   \textcolor{comment}{/*    bitmap\_left       :: The bitmap's left bearing expressed in        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1611   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         integer pixels.  Only valid if the format is  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1612   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_BITMAP, this is, if the      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1613   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         glyph slot contains a bitmap.                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1614   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1615   \textcolor{comment}{/*    bitmap\_top        :: The bitmap's top bearing expressed in integer */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1616   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         pixels.  Remember that this is the distance   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1617   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         from the baseline to the top-\/most glyph       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1618   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         scanline, upwards y\string~coordinates being         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1619   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         *positive*.                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1620   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1621   \textcolor{comment}{/*    outline           :: The outline descriptor for the current glyph  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1622   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         image if its format is                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1623   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_OUTLINE.  Once a glyph is    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1624   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         loaded, `outline' can be transformed,         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1625   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         distorted, embolded, etc.  However, it must   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1626   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         not be freed.                                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1627   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1628   \textcolor{comment}{/*    num\_subglyphs     :: The number of subglyphs in a composite glyph. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1629   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         This field is only valid for the composite    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1630   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         glyph format that should normally only be     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1631   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         loaded with the @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_RECURSE flag.     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1632   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1633   \textcolor{comment}{/*    subglyphs         :: An array of subglyph descriptors for          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1634   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         composite glyphs.  There are `num\_subglyphs'  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1635   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         elements in there.  Currently internal to     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1636   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         FreeType.                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1637   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1638   \textcolor{comment}{/*    control\_data      :: Certain font drivers can also return the      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1639   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         control data for a given glyph image (e.g.    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1640   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         TrueType bytecode, Type\string~1 charstrings, etc.). */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1641   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         This field is a pointer to such data.         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1642   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1643   \textcolor{comment}{/*    control\_len       :: This is the length in bytes of the control    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1644   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         data.                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1645   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1646   \textcolor{comment}{/*    other             :: Really wicked formats can use this pointer to */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1647   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         present their own glyph image to client       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1648   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         applications.  Note that the application      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1649   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         needs to know about the image format.         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1650   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1651   \textcolor{comment}{/*    lsb\_delta         :: The difference between hinted and unhinted    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1652   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         left side bearing while autohinting is        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1653   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         active.  Zero otherwise.                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1654   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1655   \textcolor{comment}{/*    rsb\_delta         :: The difference between hinted and unhinted    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1656   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         right side bearing while autohinting is       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1657   \textcolor{comment}{/*                         active.  Zero otherwise.                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1658   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1659   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1660   \textcolor{comment}{/*    If @FT\_Load\_Glyph is called with default flags (see                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1661   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_LOAD\_DEFAULT) the glyph image is loaded in the glyph slot in   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1662   \textcolor{comment}{/*    its native format (e.g., an outline glyph for TrueType and Type\string~1  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1663   \textcolor{comment}{/*    formats).                                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1664   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1665   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This image can later be converted into a bitmap by calling         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1666   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Render\_Glyph.  This function finds the current renderer for    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1667   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the native image's format, then invokes it.                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1668   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1669   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The renderer is in charge of transforming the native image through */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1670   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the slot's face transformation fields, then converting it into a   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1671   \textcolor{comment}{/*    bitmap that is returned in `slot-\/>bitmap'.                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1672   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1673   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Note that `slot-\/>bitmap\_left' and `slot-\/>bitmap\_top' are also used */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1674   \textcolor{comment}{/*    to specify the position of the bitmap relative to the current pen  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1675   \textcolor{comment}{/*    position (e.g., coordinates (0,0) on the baseline).  Of course,    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1676   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `slot-\/>format' is also changed to @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_BITMAP.         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1677   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1678   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1679   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Here a small pseudo code fragment that shows how to use            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1680   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `lsb\_delta' and `rsb\_delta':                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1681   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1682   \textcolor{comment}{/*    \{                                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1683   \textcolor{comment}{/*      FT\_Pos  origin\_x       = 0;                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1684   \textcolor{comment}{/*      FT\_Pos  prev\_rsb\_delta = 0;                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1685   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1686   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1687   \textcolor{comment}{/*      for all glyphs do                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1688   \textcolor{comment}{/*        <compute kern between current and previous glyph and add it to */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1689   \textcolor{comment}{/*         `origin\_x'>                                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1690   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1691   \textcolor{comment}{/*        <load glyph with `FT\_Load\_Glyph'>                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1692   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1693   \textcolor{comment}{/*        if ( prev\_rsb\_delta -\/ face-\/>glyph-\/>lsb\_delta >= 32 )           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1694   \textcolor{comment}{/*          origin\_x -\/= 64;                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1695   \textcolor{comment}{/*        else if ( prev\_rsb\_delta -\/ face-\/>glyph-\/>lsb\_delta < -\/32 )      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1696   \textcolor{comment}{/*          origin\_x += 64;                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1697   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1698   \textcolor{comment}{/*        prev\_rsb\_delta = face-\/>glyph-\/>rsb\_delta;                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1699   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1700   \textcolor{comment}{/*        <save glyph image, or render glyph, or ...>                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1701   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1702   \textcolor{comment}{/*        origin\_x += face-\/>glyph-\/>advance.x;                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1703   \textcolor{comment}{/*      endfor                                                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1704   \textcolor{comment}{/*    \}                                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1705   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1706   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct  }\mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__GlyphSlotRec__}{FT\_GlyphSlotRec\_}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1707   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1708     FT\_Library        library;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1709     \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}           face;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1710     \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__GlyphSlotRec__}{FT\_GlyphSlot}}      next;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1711     FT\_UInt           reserved;       \textcolor{comment}{/* retained for binary compatibility */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1712     \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Generic__}{FT\_Generic}}        \textcolor{keyword}{generic};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1713 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1714     FT\_Glyph\_Metrics  metrics;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1715     FT\_Fixed          linearHoriAdvance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1716     FT\_Fixed          linearVertAdvance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1717     \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Vector__}{FT\_Vector}}         advance;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1718 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1719     FT\_Glyph\_Format   format;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1720 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1721     \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Bitmap__}{FT\_Bitmap}}         bitmap;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1722     FT\_Int            bitmap\_left;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1723     FT\_Int            bitmap\_top;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1724 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1725     \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Outline__}{FT\_Outline}}        outline;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1726 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1727     FT\_UInt           num\_subglyphs;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1728     FT\_SubGlyph       subglyphs;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1729 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1730     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*             control\_data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1731     \textcolor{keywordtype}{long}              control\_len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1732 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1733     FT\_Pos            lsb\_delta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1734     FT\_Pos            rsb\_delta;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1735 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1736     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*             other;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1737 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1738     FT\_Slot\_Internal  internal;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1739 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1740   \} \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__GlyphSlotRec__}{FT\_GlyphSlotRec}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{1767   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1768   \textcolor{comment}{/*    In case you want to provide your own memory allocating routines,   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1769   \textcolor{comment}{/*    use @FT\_New\_Library instead, followed by a call to                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1770   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Add\_Default\_Modules (or a series of calls to @FT\_Add\_Module).  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1771   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1772   \textcolor{comment}{/*    For multi-\/threading applications each thread should have its own   */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1774   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1775   \textcolor{comment}{/*    If you need reference-\/counting (cf. @FT\_Reference\_Library), use    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1776   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_New\_Library and @FT\_Done\_Library.                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1777   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1801 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1802   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1803   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Enum>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1804   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_OPEN\_XXX                                                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1805   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1806   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1807   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A list of bit-\/field constants used within the `flags' field of the */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1808   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Open\_Args structure.                                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1809   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1810   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Values>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1811   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_OPEN\_MEMORY   :: This is a memory-\/based stream.                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1812   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1813   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_OPEN\_STREAM   :: Copy the stream from the `stream' field.       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1814   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1815   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_OPEN\_PATHNAME :: Create a new input stream from a C\string~path        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1816   \textcolor{comment}{/*                        name.                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1817   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1818   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_OPEN\_DRIVER   :: Use the `driver' field.                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1819   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1820   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_OPEN\_PARAMS   :: Use the `num\_params' and `params' fields.      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1821   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1822   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1823   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The `FT\_OPEN\_MEMORY', `FT\_OPEN\_STREAM', and `FT\_OPEN\_PATHNAME'     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1824   \textcolor{comment}{/*    flags are mutually exclusive.                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1825   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1826 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_OPEN\_MEMORY    0x1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1827 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_OPEN\_STREAM    0x2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1828 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_OPEN\_PATHNAME  0x4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1829 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_OPEN\_DRIVER    0x8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1830 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_OPEN\_PARAMS    0x10}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1831 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1832 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1833   \textcolor{comment}{/* these constants are deprecated; use the corresponding `FT\_OPEN\_XXX' */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1834   \textcolor{comment}{/* values instead                                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1835 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ft\_open\_memory    FT\_OPEN\_MEMORY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1836 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ft\_open\_stream    FT\_OPEN\_STREAM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1837 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ft\_open\_pathname  FT\_OPEN\_PATHNAME}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1838 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ft\_open\_driver    FT\_OPEN\_DRIVER}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1839 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ft\_open\_params    FT\_OPEN\_PARAMS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1840 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1841 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1842 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1843   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1844   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Struct>                                                              */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1849   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Open\_Face.                                                     */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1853   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1854   \textcolor{comment}{/*    data :: A pointer to the parameter data.                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1855   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1856   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1863     FT\_Pointer  data;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1864 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1865   \} \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Parameter__}{FT\_Parameter}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1866 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1867 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1868 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1869   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1870   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Struct>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1871   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Open\_Args                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1872   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1873   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1874   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A structure used to indicate how to open a new font file or        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1875   \textcolor{comment}{/*    stream.  A pointer to such a structure can be used as a parameter  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1876   \textcolor{comment}{/*    for the functions @FT\_Open\_Face and @FT\_Attach\_Stream.             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1877   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1878   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Fields>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1879   \textcolor{comment}{/*    flags       :: A set of bit flags indicating how to use the        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1880   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   structure.                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1881   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1882   \textcolor{comment}{/*    memory\_base :: The first byte of the file in memory.               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1883   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1884   \textcolor{comment}{/*    memory\_size :: The size in bytes of the file in memory.            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1885   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1886   \textcolor{comment}{/*    pathname    :: A pointer to an 8-\/bit file pathname.                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1887   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1888   \textcolor{comment}{/*    stream      :: A handle to a source stream object.                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1889   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1890   \textcolor{comment}{/*    driver      :: This field is exclusively used by @FT\_Open\_Face;    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1891   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   it simply specifies the font driver to use to open  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1892   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   the face.  If set to\string~0, FreeType tries to load the  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1893   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   face with each one of the drivers in its list.      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1894   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1895   \textcolor{comment}{/*    num\_params  :: The number of extra parameters.                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1896   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1897   \textcolor{comment}{/*    params      :: Extra parameters passed to the font driver when     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1898   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   opening a new face.                                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1899   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1900   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1901   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The stream type is determined by the contents of `flags' that      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1902   \textcolor{comment}{/*    are tested in the following order by @FT\_Open\_Face:                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1903   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1904   \textcolor{comment}{/*    If the @FT\_OPEN\_MEMORY bit is set, assume that this is a           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1905   \textcolor{comment}{/*    memory file of `memory\_size' bytes, located at `memory\_address'.   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1906   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The data are are not copied, and the client is responsible for     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1907   \textcolor{comment}{/*    releasing and destroying them \_after\_ the corresponding call to    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1908   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Done\_Face.                                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1909   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1910   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Otherwise, if the @FT\_OPEN\_STREAM bit is set, assume that a        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1911   \textcolor{comment}{/*    custom input stream `stream' is used.                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1912   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1913   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Otherwise, if the @FT\_OPEN\_PATHNAME bit is set, assume that this   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1914   \textcolor{comment}{/*    is a normal file and use `pathname' to open it.                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1915   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1916   \textcolor{comment}{/*    If the @FT\_OPEN\_DRIVER bit is set, @FT\_Open\_Face only tries to     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1917   \textcolor{comment}{/*    open the file with the driver whose handler is in `driver'.        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1918   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1919   \textcolor{comment}{/*    If the @FT\_OPEN\_PARAMS bit is set, the parameters given by         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1920   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `num\_params' and `params' is used.  They are ignored otherwise.    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1921   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1922   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Ideally, both the `pathname' and `params' fields should be tagged  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1923   \textcolor{comment}{/*    as `const'; this is missing for API backwards compatibility.  In   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1924   \textcolor{comment}{/*    other words, applications should treat them as read-\/only.          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1925   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1926   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct  }\mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Open__Args__}{FT\_Open\_Args\_}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1927   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1928     FT\_UInt         flags;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1929     \textcolor{keyword}{const} FT\_Byte*  memory\_base;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1930     FT\_Long         memory\_size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1931     FT\_String*      pathname;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1932     \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__StreamRec__}{FT\_Stream}}       stream;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1933     FT\_Module       driver;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1934     FT\_Int          num\_params;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1935     \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Parameter__}{FT\_Parameter}}*   params;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1936 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1937   \} \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Open__Args__}{FT\_Open\_Args}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1938 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1939 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2015 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2016   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2017   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2018   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Open\_Face                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2019   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2020   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2021   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Create a face object from a given resource described by            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2022   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Open\_Args.                                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2023   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2024   \textcolor{comment}{/* <InOut>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2025   \textcolor{comment}{/*    library    :: A handle to the library resource.                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2026   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2027   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2029   \textcolor{comment}{/*                  be filled by the caller.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2030   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2031   \textcolor{comment}{/*    face\_index :: The index of the face within the font.  The first    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2032   \textcolor{comment}{/*                  face has index\string~0.                                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2033   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2034   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Output>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2035   \textcolor{comment}{/*    aface      :: A handle to a new face object.  If `face\_index' is   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2036   \textcolor{comment}{/*                  greater than or equal to zero, it must be non-\/NULL.  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2037   \textcolor{comment}{/*                  See note below.                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2038   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2039   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2040   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FreeType error code.  0\string~means success.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2041   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2042   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2043   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Unlike FreeType 1.x, this function automatically creates a glyph   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2044   \textcolor{comment}{/*    slot for the face object that can be accessed directly through     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2045   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `face-\/>glyph'.                                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2046   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2047   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Open\_Face can be used to quickly check whether the font         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2048   \textcolor{comment}{/*    format of a given font resource is supported by FreeType.  If the  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2049   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `face\_index' field is negative, the function's return value is\string~0   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2050   \textcolor{comment}{/*    if the font format is recognized, or non-\/zero otherwise;           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2051   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the function returns a more or less empty face handle in `*aface'  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2052   \textcolor{comment}{/*    (if `aface' isn't NULL).  The only useful field in this special    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2053   \textcolor{comment}{/*    case is `face-\/>num\_faces' that gives the number of faces within    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2054   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the font file.  After examination, the returned @FT\_Face structure */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2055   \textcolor{comment}{/*    should be deallocated with a call to @FT\_Done\_Face.                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2056   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2057   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Each new face object created with this function also owns a        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2058   \textcolor{comment}{/*    default @FT\_Size object, accessible as `face-\/>size'.               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2059   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2060   \textcolor{comment}{/*    One @FT\_Library instance can have multiple face objects, this is,  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2061   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Open\_Face and its siblings can be called multiple times using  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2062   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the same `library' argument.                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2063   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2064   \textcolor{comment}{/*    See the discussion of reference counters in the description of     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2065   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Reference\_Face.                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2066   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2067   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_Error )}
\DoxyCodeLine{2068   FT\_Open\_Face( FT\_Library           library,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2069                 \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Open__Args__}{FT\_Open\_Args}}*  args,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2070                 FT\_Long              face\_index,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2071                 \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}             *aface );}
\DoxyCodeLine{2072 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2073 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2101   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2102   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `Attach' data to a face object.  Normally, this is used to read    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2103   \textcolor{comment}{/*    additional information for the face object.  For example, you can  */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2112   \textcolor{comment}{/*                  the caller.                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2113   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2114   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2115   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FreeType error code.  0\string~means success.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2116   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2117   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2118   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The meaning of the `attach' (i.e., what really happens when the    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2119   \textcolor{comment}{/*    new file is read) is not fixed by FreeType itself.  It really      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2120   \textcolor{comment}{/*    depends on the font format (and thus the font driver).             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2121   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2122   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Client applications are expected to know what they are doing       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2123   \textcolor{comment}{/*    when invoking this function.  Most drivers simply do not implement */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2124   \textcolor{comment}{/*    file attachments.                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2125   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2126   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_Error )}

\DoxyCodeLine{2137   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A counter gets initialized to\string~1 at the time an @FT\_Face structure  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2138   \textcolor{comment}{/*    is created.  This function increments the counter.  @FT\_Done\_Face  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2139   \textcolor{comment}{/*    then only destroys a face if the counter is\string~1, otherwise it simply */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2140   \textcolor{comment}{/*    decrements the counter.                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2141   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2142   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This function helps in managing life-\/cycles of structures that     */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2204 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2205   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2206   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Enum>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2207   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Size\_Request\_Type                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2208   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2209   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2210   \textcolor{comment}{/*    An enumeration type that lists the supported size request types.   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2211   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2212   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Values>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2213   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_NOMINAL ::                                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2214   \textcolor{comment}{/*      The nominal size.  The `units\_per\_EM' field of @FT\_FaceRec is    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2215   \textcolor{comment}{/*      used to determine both scaling values.                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2216   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2217   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_REAL\_DIM ::                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2218   \textcolor{comment}{/*      The real dimension.  The sum of the the `ascender' and (minus    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2219   \textcolor{comment}{/*      of) the `descender' fields of @FT\_FaceRec are used to determine  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2220   \textcolor{comment}{/*      both scaling values.                                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2221   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2222   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_BBOX ::                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2223   \textcolor{comment}{/*      The font bounding box.  The width and height of the `bbox' field */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2224   \textcolor{comment}{/*      of @FT\_FaceRec are used to determine the horizontal and vertical */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2225   \textcolor{comment}{/*      scaling value, respectively.                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2226   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2227   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_CELL ::                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2228   \textcolor{comment}{/*      The `max\_advance\_width' field of @FT\_FaceRec is used to          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2229   \textcolor{comment}{/*      determine the horizontal scaling value; the vertical scaling     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2230   \textcolor{comment}{/*      value is determined the same way as                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2231   \textcolor{comment}{/*      @FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_REAL\_DIM does.  Finally, both scaling      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2232   \textcolor{comment}{/*      values are set to the smaller one.  This type is useful if you   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2233   \textcolor{comment}{/*      want to specify the font size for, say, a window of a given      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2234   \textcolor{comment}{/*      dimension and 80x24 cells.                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2235   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2236   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_SCALES ::                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2237   \textcolor{comment}{/*      Specify the scaling values directly.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2238   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2239   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2240   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The above descriptions only apply to scalable formats.  For bitmap */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2241   \textcolor{comment}{/*    formats, the behaviour is up to the driver.                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2242   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2243   \textcolor{comment}{/*    See the note section of @FT\_Size\_Metrics if you wonder how size    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2244   \textcolor{comment}{/*    requesting relates to scaling values.                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2245   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2246   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{enum}  FT\_Size\_Request\_Type\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{2247   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2248     FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_NOMINAL,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2249     FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_REAL\_DIM,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2250     FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_BBOX,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2251     FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_CELL,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2252     FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_SCALES,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2253 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2254     FT\_SIZE\_REQUEST\_TYPE\_MAX}
\DoxyCodeLine{2255 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2256   \} FT\_Size\_Request\_Type;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2257 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2258 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2264   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2265   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A structure used to model a size request.                          */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2278   \textcolor{comment}{/*    vertResolution :: The vertical resolution.  If set to zero,        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2279   \textcolor{comment}{/*                      `height' is treated as a 26.6 fractional pixel   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2280   \textcolor{comment}{/*                      value.                                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2281   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2282   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2283   \textcolor{comment}{/*    If `width' is zero, then the horizontal scaling value is set equal */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2284   \textcolor{comment}{/*    to the vertical scaling value, and vice versa.                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2285   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2286   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct  }\mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Size__RequestRec__}{FT\_Size\_RequestRec\_}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2292     FT\_UInt               vertResolution;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2293 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2327   \textcolor{comment}{/*    request, you should not rely on this if you intend to select a     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2328   \textcolor{comment}{/*    particular bitmap strike.  Use @FT\_Select\_Size instead in that     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2329   \textcolor{comment}{/*    case.                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2330   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2331   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The relation between the requested size and the resulting glyph    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2332   \textcolor{comment}{/*    size is dependent entirely on how the size is defined in the       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2333   \textcolor{comment}{/*    source face.  The font designer chooses the final size of each     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2334   \textcolor{comment}{/*    glyph relative to this size.  For more information refer to        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2335   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `http://www.freetype.org/freetype2/docs/glyphs/glyphs-\/2.html'      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2336   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2337   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Don't use this function if you are using the FreeType cache API.   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2338   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2347   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Set\_Char\_Size                                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2348   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2349   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2350   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This function calls @FT\_Request\_Size to request the nominal size   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2351   \textcolor{comment}{/*    (in points).                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2352   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2353   \textcolor{comment}{/* <InOut>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2354   \textcolor{comment}{/*    face            :: A handle to a target face object.               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2355   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2356   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2357   \textcolor{comment}{/*    char\_width      :: The nominal width, in 26.6 fractional points.   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2358   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2359   \textcolor{comment}{/*    char\_height     :: The nominal height, in 26.6 fractional points.  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2360   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2361   \textcolor{comment}{/*    horz\_resolution :: The horizontal resolution in dpi.               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2362   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2363   \textcolor{comment}{/*    vert\_resolution :: The vertical resolution in dpi.                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2364   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2365   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2366   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FreeType error code.  0\string~means success.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2367   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2368   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2369   \textcolor{comment}{/*    If either the character width or height is zero, it is set equal   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2370   \textcolor{comment}{/*    to the other value.                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2371   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2372   \textcolor{comment}{/*    If either the horizontal or vertical resolution is zero, it is set */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2373   \textcolor{comment}{/*    equal to the other value.                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2374   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2375   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A character width or height smaller than 1pt is set to 1pt; if     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2376   \textcolor{comment}{/*    both resolution values are zero, they are set to 72dpi.            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2377   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2378   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Don't use this function if you are using the FreeType cache API.   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2379   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2380   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_Error )}
\DoxyCodeLine{2381   FT\_Set\_Char\_Size( \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}     face,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2382                     FT\_F26Dot6  char\_width,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2383                     FT\_F26Dot6  char\_height,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2384                     FT\_UInt     horz\_resolution,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2385                     FT\_UInt     vert\_resolution );}
\DoxyCodeLine{2386 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2387 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2388 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2421 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2422   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2423   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2424   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Load\_Glyph                                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2425   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2426   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2427   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A function used to load a single glyph into the glyph slot of a    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2428   \textcolor{comment}{/*    face object.                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2429   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2430   \textcolor{comment}{/* <InOut>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2431   \textcolor{comment}{/*    face        :: A handle to the target face object where the glyph  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2432   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   is loaded.                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2433   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2434   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2435   \textcolor{comment}{/*    glyph\_index :: The index of the glyph in the font file.  For       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2436   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   CID-\/keyed fonts (either in PS or in CFF format)     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2437   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   this argument specifies the CID value.              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2438   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2439   \textcolor{comment}{/*    load\_flags  :: A flag indicating what to load for this glyph.  The */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2440   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   @FT\_LOAD\_XXX constants can be used to control the   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2441   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   glyph loading process (e.g., whether the outline    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2442   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   should be scaled, whether to load bitmaps or not,   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2443   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   whether to hint the outline, etc).                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2444   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2445   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2446   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FreeType error code.  0\string~means success.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2447   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2448   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2449   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The loaded glyph may be transformed.  See @FT\_Set\_Transform for    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2450   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the details.                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2451   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2452   \textcolor{comment}{/*    For subsetted CID-\/keyed fonts, `FT\_Err\_Invalid\_Argument' is        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2453   \textcolor{comment}{/*    returned for invalid CID values (this is, for CID values that      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2454   \textcolor{comment}{/*    don't have a corresponding glyph in the font).  See the discussion */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2455   \textcolor{comment}{/*    of the @FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_CID\_KEYED flag for more details.              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2456   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2457   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_Error )}
\DoxyCodeLine{2458   FT\_Load\_Glyph( \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}   face,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2459                  FT\_UInt   glyph\_index,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2460                  FT\_Int32  load\_flags );}
\DoxyCodeLine{2461 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2463 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2464   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2465   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2466   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Load\_Char                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2467   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2468   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
