\DoxyCodeLine{2474   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   is loaded.                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2475   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2476   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2477   \textcolor{comment}{/*    char\_code   :: The glyph's character code, according to the        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2478   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   current charmap used in the face.                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2479   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2480   \textcolor{comment}{/*    load\_flags  :: A flag indicating what to load for this glyph.  The */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2481   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   @FT\_LOAD\_XXX constants can be used to control the   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2482   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   glyph loading process (e.g., whether the outline    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2483   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   should be scaled, whether to load bitmaps or not,   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2484   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   whether to hint the outline, etc).                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2485   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2486   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2488   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2489   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2490   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This function simply calls @FT\_Get\_Char\_Index and @FT\_Load\_Glyph.  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2491   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2492   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_Error )}
\DoxyCodeLine{2493   FT\_Load\_Char( \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}   face,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2494                 FT\_ULong  char\_code,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2495                 FT\_Int32  load\_flags );}
\DoxyCodeLine{2496 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2497 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2498 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2499 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2500 \textcolor{comment}{   * @enum:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2501 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2502 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2503 \textcolor{comment}{   * @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2504 \textcolor{comment}{   *   A list of bit-\/field constants used with @FT\_Load\_Glyph to indicate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2505 \textcolor{comment}{   *   what kind of operations to perform during glyph loading.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2506 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2507 \textcolor{comment}{   * @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2508 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_DEFAULT ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2509 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Corresponding to\string~0, this value is used as the default glyph load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2510 \textcolor{comment}{   *     operation.  In this case, the following happens:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2511 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2512 \textcolor{comment}{   *     1. FreeType looks for a bitmap for the glyph corresponding to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2513 \textcolor{comment}{   *        face's current size.  If one is found, the function returns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2514 \textcolor{comment}{   *        The bitmap data can be accessed from the glyph slot (see note}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2515 \textcolor{comment}{   *        below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2516 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2517 \textcolor{comment}{   *     2. If no embedded bitmap is searched or found, FreeType looks for a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2518 \textcolor{comment}{   *        scalable outline.  If one is found, it is loaded from the font}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2519 \textcolor{comment}{   *        file, scaled to device pixels, then `hinted' to the pixel grid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2520 \textcolor{comment}{   *        in order to optimize it.  The outline data can be accessed from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2521 \textcolor{comment}{   *        the glyph slot (see note below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2522 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2523 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Note that by default, the glyph loader doesn't render outlines into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2524 \textcolor{comment}{   *     bitmaps.  The following flags are used to modify this default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2525 \textcolor{comment}{   *     behaviour to more specific and useful cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2526 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2527 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2528 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Don't scale the loaded outline glyph but keep it in font units.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2529 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2530 \textcolor{comment}{   *     This flag implies @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING and @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_BITMAP, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2531 \textcolor{comment}{   *     unsets @FT\_LOAD\_RENDER.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2532 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2533 \textcolor{comment}{   *     If the font is `tricky' (see @FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_TRICKY for more), using}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2534 \textcolor{comment}{   *     FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE usually yields meaningless outlines because the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2535 \textcolor{comment}{   *     subglyphs must be scaled and positioned with hinting instructions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2536 \textcolor{comment}{   *     This can be solved by loading the font without FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2537 \textcolor{comment}{   *     setting the character size to `font-\/>units\_per\_EM'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2538 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2539 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2540 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Disable hinting.  This generally generates `blurrier' bitmap glyphs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2541 \textcolor{comment}{   *     when the glyph are rendered in any of the anti-\/aliased modes.  See}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2542 \textcolor{comment}{   *     also the note below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2543 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2544 \textcolor{comment}{   *     This flag is implied by @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2545 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2546 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_RENDER ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2547 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Call @FT\_Render\_Glyph after the glyph is loaded.  By default, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2548 \textcolor{comment}{   *     glyph is rendered in @FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL mode.  This can be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2549 \textcolor{comment}{   *     overridden by @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX or @FT\_LOAD\_MONOCHROME.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2550 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2551 \textcolor{comment}{   *     This flag is unset by @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2552 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2553 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_NO\_BITMAP ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2554 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Ignore bitmap strikes when loading.  Bitmap-\/only fonts ignore this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2555 \textcolor{comment}{   *     flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2556 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2557 \textcolor{comment}{   *     @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE always sets this flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2558 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2559 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_VERTICAL\_LAYOUT ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2560 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Load the glyph for vertical text layout.  In particular, the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2561 \textcolor{comment}{   *     `advance' value in the @FT\_GlyphSlotRec structure is set to the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2562 \textcolor{comment}{   *     `vertAdvance' value of the `metrics' field.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2563 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2564 \textcolor{comment}{   *     In case @FT\_HAS\_VERTICAL doesn't return true, you shouldn't use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2565 \textcolor{comment}{   *     this flag currently.  Reason is that in this case vertical metrics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2566 \textcolor{comment}{   *     get synthesized, and those values are not always consistent across}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2567 \textcolor{comment}{   *     various font formats.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2568 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2569 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2570 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Indicates that the auto-\/hinter is preferred over the font's native}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2571 \textcolor{comment}{   *     hinter.  See also the note below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2572 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2573 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_PEDANTIC ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2574 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Indicates that the font driver should perform pedantic verifications}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2575 \textcolor{comment}{   *     during glyph loading.  This is mostly used to detect broken glyphs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2576 \textcolor{comment}{   *     in fonts.  By default, FreeType tries to handle broken fonts also.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2577 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2578 \textcolor{comment}{   *     In particular, errors from the TrueType bytecode engine are not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2579 \textcolor{comment}{   *     passed to the application if this flag is not set; this might}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2580 \textcolor{comment}{   *     result in partially hinted or distorted glyphs in case a glyph's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2581 \textcolor{comment}{   *     bytecode is buggy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2582 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2583 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_NO\_RECURSE ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2584 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Indicate that the font driver should not load composite glyphs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2585 \textcolor{comment}{   *     recursively.  Instead, it should set the `num\_subglyph' and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2586 \textcolor{comment}{   *     `subglyphs' values of the glyph slot accordingly, and set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2587 \textcolor{comment}{   *     `glyph-\/>format' to @FT\_GLYPH\_FORMAT\_COMPOSITE.  The description of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2588 \textcolor{comment}{   *     subglyphs can then be accessed with @FT\_Get\_SubGlyph\_Info.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2589 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2590 \textcolor{comment}{   *     This flag implies @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE and @FT\_LOAD\_IGNORE\_TRANSFORM.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2591 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2592 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_IGNORE\_TRANSFORM ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2593 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Indicates that the transform matrix set by @FT\_Set\_Transform should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2594 \textcolor{comment}{   *     be ignored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2595 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2596 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_MONOCHROME ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2597 \textcolor{comment}{   *     This flag is used with @FT\_LOAD\_RENDER to indicate that you want to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2598 \textcolor{comment}{   *     render an outline glyph to a 1-\/bit monochrome bitmap glyph, with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2599 \textcolor{comment}{   *     8\string~pixels packed into each byte of the bitmap data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2600 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2601 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Note that this has no effect on the hinting algorithm used.  You}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2602 \textcolor{comment}{   *     should rather use @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO so that the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2603 \textcolor{comment}{   *     monochrome-\/optimized hinting algorithm is used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2604 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2605 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_LINEAR\_DESIGN ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2606 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Indicates that the `linearHoriAdvance' and `linearVertAdvance'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2607 \textcolor{comment}{   *     fields of @FT\_GlyphSlotRec should be kept in font units.  See}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2608 \textcolor{comment}{   *     @FT\_GlyphSlotRec for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2609 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2610 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_NO\_AUTOHINT ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2611 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Disable auto-\/hinter.  See also the note below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2612 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2613 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_COLOR ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2614 \textcolor{comment}{   *     This flag is used to request loading of color embedded-\/bitmap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2615 \textcolor{comment}{   *     images.  The resulting color bitmaps, if available, will have the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2616 \textcolor{comment}{   *     @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_BGRA format.  When the flag is not used and color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2617 \textcolor{comment}{   *     bitmaps are found, they will be converted to 256-\/level gray}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2618 \textcolor{comment}{   *     bitmaps transparently.  Those bitmaps will be in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2619 \textcolor{comment}{   *     @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_GRAY format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2620 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2621 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_CROP\_BITMAP ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2622 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Ignored.  Deprecated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2623 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2624 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_IGNORE\_GLOBAL\_ADVANCE\_WIDTH ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2625 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Ignored.  Deprecated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2626 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2627 \textcolor{comment}{   * @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2628 \textcolor{comment}{   *   By default, hinting is enabled and the font's native hinter (see}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2629 \textcolor{comment}{   *   @FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_HINTER) is preferred over the auto-\/hinter.  You can}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2630 \textcolor{comment}{   *   disable hinting by setting @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING or change the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2631 \textcolor{comment}{   *   precedence by setting @FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT.  You can also set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2632 \textcolor{comment}{   *   @FT\_LOAD\_NO\_AUTOHINT in case you don't want the auto-\/hinter to be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2633 \textcolor{comment}{   *   used at all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2634 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2635 \textcolor{comment}{   *   See the description of @FT\_FACE\_FLAG\_TRICKY for a special exception}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2636 \textcolor{comment}{   *   (affecting only a handful of Asian fonts).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2637 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2638 \textcolor{comment}{   *   Besides deciding which hinter to use, you can also decide which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2639 \textcolor{comment}{   *   hinting algorithm to use.  See @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2640 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2641 \textcolor{comment}{   *   Note that the auto-\/hinter needs a valid Unicode cmap (either a native}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2642 \textcolor{comment}{   *   one or synthesized by FreeType) for producing correct results.  If a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2643 \textcolor{comment}{   *   font provides an incorrect mapping (for example, assigning the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2644 \textcolor{comment}{   *   character code U+005A, LATIN CAPITAL LETTER Z, to a glyph depicting a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2645 \textcolor{comment}{   *   mathematical integral sign), the auto-\/hinter might produce useless}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2646 \textcolor{comment}{   *   results.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2647 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2648 \textcolor{comment}{   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2649 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_DEFAULT                      0x0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2650 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_NO\_SCALE                     ( 1L << 0 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2651 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_NO\_HINTING                   ( 1L << 1 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2652 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_RENDER                       ( 1L << 2 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2653 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_NO\_BITMAP                    ( 1L << 3 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2654 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_VERTICAL\_LAYOUT              ( 1L << 4 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2655 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT               ( 1L << 5 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2656 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_CROP\_BITMAP                  ( 1L << 6 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2657 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_PEDANTIC                     ( 1L << 7 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2658 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_IGNORE\_GLOBAL\_ADVANCE\_WIDTH  ( 1L << 9 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2659 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_NO\_RECURSE                   ( 1L << 10 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2660 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_IGNORE\_TRANSFORM             ( 1L << 11 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2661 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_MONOCHROME                   ( 1L << 12 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2662 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_LINEAR\_DESIGN                ( 1L << 13 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2663 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_NO\_AUTOHINT                  ( 1L << 15 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2664   \textcolor{comment}{/* Bits 16..19 are used by `FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_' */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2665 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_COLOR                        ( 1L << 20 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2666 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2667   \textcolor{comment}{/* */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2668 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2669   \textcolor{comment}{/* used internally only by certain font drivers! */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2670 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_ADVANCE\_ONLY                 ( 1L << 8 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2671 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_SBITS\_ONLY                   ( 1L << 14 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2672 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2673 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2674 \textcolor{comment}{  /**************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2675 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2676 \textcolor{comment}{   * @enum:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2677 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2678 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2679 \textcolor{comment}{   * @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2680 \textcolor{comment}{   *   A list of values that are used to select a specific hinting algorithm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2681 \textcolor{comment}{   *   to use by the hinter.  You should OR one of these values to your}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2682 \textcolor{comment}{   *   `load\_flags' when calling @FT\_Load\_Glyph.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2683 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2684 \textcolor{comment}{   *   Note that font's native hinters may ignore the hinting algorithm you}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2685 \textcolor{comment}{   *   have specified (e.g., the TrueType bytecode interpreter).  You can set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2686 \textcolor{comment}{   *   @FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT to ensure that the auto-\/hinter is used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2687 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2688 \textcolor{comment}{   *   Also note that @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LIGHT is an exception, in that it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2689 \textcolor{comment}{   *   always implies @FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2690 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2691 \textcolor{comment}{   * @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2692 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_NORMAL ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2693 \textcolor{comment}{   *     This corresponds to the default hinting algorithm, optimized for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2694 \textcolor{comment}{   *     standard gray-\/level rendering.  For monochrome output, use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2695 \textcolor{comment}{   *     @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2696 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2697 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LIGHT ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2698 \textcolor{comment}{   *     A lighter hinting algorithm for non-\/monochrome modes.  Many}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2699 \textcolor{comment}{   *     generated glyphs are more fuzzy but better resemble its original}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2700 \textcolor{comment}{   *     shape.  A bit like rendering on Mac OS\string~X.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2701 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2702 \textcolor{comment}{   *     As a special exception, this target implies @FT\_LOAD\_FORCE\_AUTOHINT.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2703 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2704 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2705 \textcolor{comment}{   *     Strong hinting algorithm that should only be used for monochrome}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2706 \textcolor{comment}{   *     output.  The result is probably unpleasant if the glyph is rendered}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2707 \textcolor{comment}{   *     in non-\/monochrome modes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2708 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2709 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LCD ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2710 \textcolor{comment}{   *     A variant of @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_NORMAL optimized for horizontally}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2711 \textcolor{comment}{   *     decimated LCD displays.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2712 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2713 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LCD\_V ::}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2714 \textcolor{comment}{   *     A variant of @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_NORMAL optimized for vertically}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2715 \textcolor{comment}{   *     decimated LCD displays.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2716 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2717 \textcolor{comment}{   * @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2718 \textcolor{comment}{   *   You should use only \_one\_ of the FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX values in your}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2719 \textcolor{comment}{   *   `load\_flags'.  They can't be ORed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2720 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2721 \textcolor{comment}{   *   If @FT\_LOAD\_RENDER is also set, the glyph is rendered in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2722 \textcolor{comment}{   *   corresponding mode (i.e., the mode that matches the used algorithm}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2723 \textcolor{comment}{   *   best).  An exeption is FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO since it implies}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2724 \textcolor{comment}{   *   @FT\_LOAD\_MONOCHROME.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2725 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2726 \textcolor{comment}{   *   You can use a hinting algorithm that doesn't correspond to the same}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2727 \textcolor{comment}{   *   rendering mode.  As an example, it is possible to use the `light'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2728 \textcolor{comment}{   *   hinting algorithm and have the results rendered in horizontal LCD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2729 \textcolor{comment}{   *   pixel mode, with code like}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2730 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2731 \textcolor{comment}{   *     \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2732 \textcolor{comment}{   *       FT\_Load\_Glyph( face, glyph\_index,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2733 \textcolor{comment}{   *                      load\_flags | FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LIGHT );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2734 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2735 \textcolor{comment}{   *       FT\_Render\_Glyph( face-\/>glyph, FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LCD );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2736 \textcolor{comment}{   *     \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2737 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2738 \textcolor{comment}{   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2739 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_( x )   ( (FT\_Int32)( (x) \& 15 ) << 16 )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2740 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2741 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_NORMAL  FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_( FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2742 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LIGHT   FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_( FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LIGHT  )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2743 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MONO    FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_( FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_MONO   )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2744 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LCD     FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_( FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LCD    )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2745 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_LCD\_V   FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_( FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LCD\_V  )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2746 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2747 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2748 \textcolor{comment}{  /**************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2749 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2750 \textcolor{comment}{   * @macro:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2751 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MODE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2752 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2753 \textcolor{comment}{   * @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2754 \textcolor{comment}{   *   Return the @FT\_Render\_Mode corresponding to a given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2755 \textcolor{comment}{   *   @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2756 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2757 \textcolor{comment}{   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2758 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_MODE( x )  ( (FT\_Render\_Mode)( ( (x) >> 16 ) \& 15 ) )}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2759 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2760 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2761 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2762   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2763   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2764   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Set\_Transform                                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2765   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2766   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2767   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A function used to set the transformation that is applied to glyph */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2768   \textcolor{comment}{/*    images when they are loaded into a glyph slot through              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2769   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Load\_Glyph.                                                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2770   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2771   \textcolor{comment}{/* <InOut>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2772   \textcolor{comment}{/*    face   :: A handle to the source face object.                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2773   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2774   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2775   \textcolor{comment}{/*    matrix :: A pointer to the transformation's 2x2 matrix.  Use\string~0 for */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2776   \textcolor{comment}{/*              the identity matrix.                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2777   \textcolor{comment}{/*    delta  :: A pointer to the translation vector.  Use\string~0 for the null */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2778   \textcolor{comment}{/*              vector.                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2779   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2780   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2781   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The transformation is only applied to scalable image formats after */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2782   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the glyph has been loaded.  It means that hinting is unaltered by  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2783   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the transformation and is performed on the character size given in */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2784   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the last call to @FT\_Set\_Char\_Size or @FT\_Set\_Pixel\_Sizes.         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2785   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2786   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Note that this also transforms the `face.glyph.advance' field, but */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2787   \textcolor{comment}{/*    *not* the values in `face.glyph.metrics'.                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2788   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2789   FT\_EXPORT( \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} )}
\DoxyCodeLine{2790   FT\_Set\_Transform( \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}     face,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2791                     \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Matrix__}{FT\_Matrix}}*  matrix,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2792                     \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__Vector__}{FT\_Vector}}*  delta );}
\DoxyCodeLine{2793 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2794 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2795 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2796   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2797   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Enum>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2798   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Render\_Mode                                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2799   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2800   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2801   \textcolor{comment}{/*    An enumeration type that lists the render modes supported by       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2802   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FreeType\string~2.  Each mode corresponds to a specific type of scanline  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2803   \textcolor{comment}{/*    conversion performed on the outline.                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2804   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2805   \textcolor{comment}{/*    For bitmap fonts and embedded bitmaps the `bitmap-\/>pixel\_mode'     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2806   \textcolor{comment}{/*    field in the @FT\_GlyphSlotRec structure gives the format of the    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2807   \textcolor{comment}{/*    returned bitmap.                                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2808   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2809   \textcolor{comment}{/*    All modes except @FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_MONO use 256 levels of opacity.   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2810   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2811   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Values>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2812   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL ::                                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2813   \textcolor{comment}{/*      This is the default render mode; it corresponds to 8-\/bit         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2814   \textcolor{comment}{/*      anti-\/aliased bitmaps.                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2815   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2816   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LIGHT ::                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2817   \textcolor{comment}{/*      This is equivalent to @FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL.  It is only        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2818   \textcolor{comment}{/*      defined as a separate value because render modes are also used   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2819   \textcolor{comment}{/*      indirectly to define hinting algorithm selectors.  See           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2820   \textcolor{comment}{/*      @FT\_LOAD\_TARGET\_XXX for details.                                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2821   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2822   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_MONO ::                                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2823   \textcolor{comment}{/*      This mode corresponds to 1-\/bit bitmaps (with 2\string~levels of         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2824   \textcolor{comment}{/*      opacity).                                                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2825   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2826   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LCD ::                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2827   \textcolor{comment}{/*      This mode corresponds to horizontal RGB and BGR sub-\/pixel        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2828   \textcolor{comment}{/*      displays like LCD screens.  It produces 8-\/bit bitmaps that are   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2829   \textcolor{comment}{/*      3\string~times the width of the original glyph outline in pixels, and   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2830   \textcolor{comment}{/*      which use the @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_LCD mode.                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2831   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2832   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LCD\_V ::                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2833   \textcolor{comment}{/*      This mode corresponds to vertical RGB and BGR sub-\/pixel displays */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2834   \textcolor{comment}{/*      (like PDA screens, rotated LCD displays, etc.).  It produces     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2835   \textcolor{comment}{/*      8-\/bit bitmaps that are 3\string~times the height of the original        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2836   \textcolor{comment}{/*      glyph outline in pixels and use the @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_LCD\_V mode.   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2837   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2838   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2839   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The LCD-\/optimized glyph bitmaps produced by FT\_Render\_Glyph can be */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2840   \textcolor{comment}{/*    filtered to reduce color-\/fringes by using @FT\_Library\_SetLcdFilter */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2841   \textcolor{comment}{/*    (not active in the default builds).  It is up to the caller to     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2842   \textcolor{comment}{/*    either call @FT\_Library\_SetLcdFilter (if available) or do the      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2843   \textcolor{comment}{/*    filtering itself.                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2844   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2845   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The selected render mode only affects vector glyphs of a font.     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2846   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Embedded bitmaps often have a different pixel mode like            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2847   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_PIXEL\_MODE\_MONO.  You can use @FT\_Bitmap\_Convert to transform  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2848   \textcolor{comment}{/*    them into 8-\/bit pixmaps.                                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2849   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2850   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{enum}  FT\_Render\_Mode\_}
\DoxyCodeLine{2851   \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2852     FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2853     FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LIGHT,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2854     FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_MONO,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2855     FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LCD,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2856     FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_LCD\_V,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2857 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2858     FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_MAX}
\DoxyCodeLine{2859 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2860   \} FT\_Render\_Mode;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2861 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2862 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2863   \textcolor{comment}{/* these constants are deprecated; use the corresponding */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2864   \textcolor{comment}{/* `FT\_Render\_Mode' values instead                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2865 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ft\_render\_mode\_normal  FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_NORMAL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2866 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ft\_render\_mode\_mono    FT\_RENDER\_MODE\_MONO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2867 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2868 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2869 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2870   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2871   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2872   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Render\_Glyph                                                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2873   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2874   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2875   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Convert a given glyph image to a bitmap.  It does so by inspecting */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2876   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the glyph image format, finding the relevant renderer, and         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2877   \textcolor{comment}{/*    invoking it.                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2878   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2879   \textcolor{comment}{/* <InOut>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2880   \textcolor{comment}{/*    slot        :: A handle to the glyph slot containing the image to  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2881   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   convert.                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2882   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2883   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2884   \textcolor{comment}{/*    render\_mode :: This is the render mode used to render the glyph    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2885   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   image into a bitmap.  See @FT\_Render\_Mode for a     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2886   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   list of possible values.                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2887   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2888   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2889   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FreeType error code.  0\string~means success.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2890   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2891   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2892   \textcolor{comment}{/*    To get meaningful results, font scaling values must be set with    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2893   \textcolor{comment}{/*    functions like @FT\_Set\_Char\_Size before calling FT\_Render\_Glyph.   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2894   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2895   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_Error )}
\DoxyCodeLine{2896   FT\_Render\_Glyph( \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__GlyphSlotRec__}{FT\_GlyphSlot}}    slot,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2897                    FT\_Render\_Mode  render\_mode );}
\DoxyCodeLine{2898 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2899 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2900 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2901   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2902   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Enum>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2903   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Kerning\_Mode                                                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2904   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2905   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2906   \textcolor{comment}{/*    An enumeration used to specify which kerning values to return in   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2907   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Get\_Kerning.                                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2908   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2909   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Values>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2910   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_KERNING\_DEFAULT  :: Return scaled and grid-\/fitted kerning       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2911   \textcolor{comment}{/*                           distances (value is\string~0).                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2912   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2913   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_KERNING\_UNFITTED :: Return scaled but un-\/grid-\/fitted kerning    */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2915   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2918   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2919   \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{enum}  FT\_Kerning\_Mode\_}

\DoxyCodeLine{2923     FT\_KERNING\_UNSCALED}

\DoxyCodeLine{2940   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2941   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Return the kerning vector between two glyphs of a same face.       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2942   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2947   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2950   \textcolor{comment}{/*    kern\_mode   :: See @FT\_Kerning\_Mode for more information.          */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2954   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Output>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2955   \textcolor{comment}{/*    akerning    :: The kerning vector.  This is either in font units   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2956   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   or in pixels (26.6 format) for scalable formats,    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2957   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   and in pixels for fixed-\/sizes formats.              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2958   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2959   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2960   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FreeType error code.  0\string~means success.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2961   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2962   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2963   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Only horizontal layouts (left-\/to-\/right \& right-\/to-\/left) are        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2964   \textcolor{comment}{/*    supported by this method.  Other layouts, or more sophisticated    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2965   \textcolor{comment}{/*    kernings, are out of the scope of this API function -\/-\/ they can be */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2966   \textcolor{comment}{/*    implemented through format-\/specific interfaces.                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2967   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3019   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Get\_Glyph\_Name                                                  */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3021   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3022   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Retrieve the ASCII name of a given glyph in a face.  This only     */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3029   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3030   \textcolor{comment}{/*    buffer\_max  :: The maximum number of bytes available in the        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3031   \textcolor{comment}{/*                   buffer.                                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3032   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3033   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Output>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3034   \textcolor{comment}{/*    buffer      :: A pointer to a target buffer where the name is      */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3036   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3037   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3038   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FreeType error code.  0\string~means success.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3039   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3040   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3041   \textcolor{comment}{/*    An error is returned if the face doesn't provide glyph names or if */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3042   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the glyph index is invalid.  In all cases of failure, the first    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3043   \textcolor{comment}{/*    byte of `buffer' is set to\string~0 to indicate an empty name.            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3044   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3045   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The glyph name is truncated to fit within the buffer if it is too  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3046   \textcolor{comment}{/*    long.  The returned string is always zero-\/terminated.              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3047   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3048   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Be aware that FreeType reorders glyph indices internally so that   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3049   \textcolor{comment}{/*    glyph index\string~0 always corresponds to the `missing glyph' (called    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3050   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `.notdef').                                                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3051   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3052   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This function always returns an error if the config macro          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3053   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `FT\_CONFIG\_OPTION\_NO\_GLYPH\_NAMES' is not defined in `ftoptions.h'. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3054   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3055   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_Error )}
\DoxyCodeLine{3056   FT\_Get\_Glyph\_Name( \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}     face,}

\DoxyCodeLine{3168 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3169   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3170   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3171   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Get\_Char\_Index                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3172   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3173   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3174   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Return the glyph index of a given character code.  This function   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3175   \textcolor{comment}{/*    uses a charmap object to do the mapping.                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3176   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3177   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3178   \textcolor{comment}{/*    face     :: A handle to the source face object.                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3179   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3180   \textcolor{comment}{/*    charcode :: The character code.                                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3181   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3182   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3183   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The glyph index.  0\string~means `undefined character code'.              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3184   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3185   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3186   \textcolor{comment}{/*    If you use FreeType to manipulate the contents of font files       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3187   \textcolor{comment}{/*    directly, be aware that the glyph index returned by this function  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3188   \textcolor{comment}{/*    doesn't always correspond to the internal indices used within the  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3189   \textcolor{comment}{/*    file.  This is done to ensure that value\string~0 always corresponds to   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3190   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the `missing glyph'.  If the first glyph is not named `.notdef',   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3191   \textcolor{comment}{/*    then for Type\string~1 and Type\string~42 fonts, `.notdef' will be moved into    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3192   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the glyph ID\string~0 position, and whatever was there will be moved to   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3193   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the position `.notdef' had.  For Type\string~1 fonts, if there is no      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3194   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `.notdef' glyph at all, then one will be created at index\string~0 and    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3195   \textcolor{comment}{/*    whatever was there will be moved to the last index -\/-\/ Type\string~42      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3196   \textcolor{comment}{/*    fonts are considered invalid under this condition.                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3197   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3198   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_UInt )}
\DoxyCodeLine{3199   FT\_Get\_Char\_Index( \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}   face,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3200                      FT\_ULong  charcode );}
\DoxyCodeLine{3201 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3202 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3203 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3204   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3205   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3206   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Get\_First\_Char                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3207   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3208   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3209   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This function is used to return the first character code in the    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3210   \textcolor{comment}{/*    current charmap of a given face.  It also returns the              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3211   \textcolor{comment}{/*    corresponding glyph index.                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3212   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3213   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3214   \textcolor{comment}{/*    face    :: A handle to the source face object.                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3215   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3216   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Output>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3217   \textcolor{comment}{/*    agindex :: Glyph index of first character code.  0\string~if charmap is   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3218   \textcolor{comment}{/*               empty.                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3219   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3220   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3221   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The charmap's first character code.                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3222   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3223   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3224   \textcolor{comment}{/*    You should use this function with @FT\_Get\_Next\_Char to be able to  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3225   \textcolor{comment}{/*    parse all character codes available in a given charmap.  The code  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3226   \textcolor{comment}{/*    should look like this:                                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3227   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3228   \textcolor{comment}{/*    \{                                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3229   \textcolor{comment}{/*      FT\_ULong  charcode;                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3230   \textcolor{comment}{/*      FT\_UInt   gindex;                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3231   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3232   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3233   \textcolor{comment}{/*      charcode = FT\_Get\_First\_Char( face, \&gindex );                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3234   \textcolor{comment}{/*      while ( gindex != 0 )                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3235   \textcolor{comment}{/*      \{                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3236   \textcolor{comment}{/*        ... do something with (charcode,gindex) pair ...               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3237   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3238   \textcolor{comment}{/*        charcode = FT\_Get\_Next\_Char( face, charcode, \&gindex );        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3239   \textcolor{comment}{/*      \}                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3240   \textcolor{comment}{/*    \}                                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3241   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3242   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Note that `*agindex' is set to\string~0 if the charmap is empty.  The     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3243   \textcolor{comment}{/*    result itself can be\string~0 in two cases: if the charmap is empty or    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3244   \textcolor{comment}{/*    if the value\string~0 is the first valid character code.                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3245   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3246   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_ULong )}
\DoxyCodeLine{3247   FT\_Get\_First\_Char( \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}   face,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3248                      FT\_UInt  *agindex );}
\DoxyCodeLine{3249 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3250 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3251 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3252   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3253   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3254   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Get\_Next\_Char                                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3255   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3256   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3257   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This function is used to return the next character code in the     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3258   \textcolor{comment}{/*    current charmap of a given face following the value `char\_code',   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3259   \textcolor{comment}{/*    as well as the corresponding glyph index.                          */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3261   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3263   \textcolor{comment}{/*    char\_code :: The starting character code.                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3264   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3265   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Output>                                                              */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3267   \textcolor{comment}{/*                 is empty.                                             */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3274   \textcolor{comment}{/*    over all character codes available in a given charmap.  See the    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275   \textcolor{comment}{/*    note for this function for a simple code example.                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3277   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Note that `*agindex' is set to\string~0 when there are no more codes in   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3278   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the charmap.                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3279   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3280   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_ULong )}

\DoxyCodeLine{3283                     FT\_UInt   *agindex );}

\DoxyCodeLine{3389 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3390   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3391   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Enum>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3392   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_FSTYPE\_XXX                                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3393   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3394   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3395   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A list of bit flags used in the `fsType' field of the OS/2 table   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3396   \textcolor{comment}{/*    in a TrueType or OpenType font and the `FSType' entry in a         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3397   \textcolor{comment}{/*    PostScript font.  These bit flags are returned by                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3398   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FT\_Get\_FSType\_Flags; they inform client applications of embedding */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3399   \textcolor{comment}{/*    and subsetting restrictions associated with a font.                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3400   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3401   \textcolor{comment}{/*    See http://www.adobe.com/devnet/acrobat/pdfs/FontPolicies.pdf for  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3402   \textcolor{comment}{/*    more details.                                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3403   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3404   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Values>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3405   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_FSTYPE\_INSTALLABLE\_EMBEDDING ::                                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3406   \textcolor{comment}{/*      Fonts with no fsType bit set may be embedded and permanently     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3407   \textcolor{comment}{/*      installed on the remote system by an application.                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3408   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3409   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_FSTYPE\_RESTRICTED\_LICENSE\_EMBEDDING ::                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3410   \textcolor{comment}{/*      Fonts that have only this bit set must not be modified, embedded */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3411   \textcolor{comment}{/*      or exchanged in any manner without first obtaining permission of */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3412   \textcolor{comment}{/*      the font software copyright owner.                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3413   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3414   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_FSTYPE\_PREVIEW\_AND\_PRINT\_EMBEDDING ::                           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3415   \textcolor{comment}{/*      If this bit is set, the font may be embedded and temporarily     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3416   \textcolor{comment}{/*      loaded on the remote system.  Documents containing Preview \&     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3417   \textcolor{comment}{/*      Print fonts must be opened `read-\/only'; no edits can be applied  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3418   \textcolor{comment}{/*      to the document.                                                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3419   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3420   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_FSTYPE\_EDITABLE\_EMBEDDING ::                                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3421   \textcolor{comment}{/*      If this bit is set, the font may be embedded but must only be    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3422   \textcolor{comment}{/*      installed temporarily on other systems.  In contrast to Preview  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3423   \textcolor{comment}{/*      \& Print fonts, documents containing editable fonts may be opened */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3424   \textcolor{comment}{/*      for reading, editing is permitted, and changes may be saved.     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3425   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3426   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_FSTYPE\_NO\_SUBSETTING ::                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3427   \textcolor{comment}{/*      If this bit is set, the font may not be subsetted prior to       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3428   \textcolor{comment}{/*      embedding.                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3429   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3430   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_FSTYPE\_BITMAP\_EMBEDDING\_ONLY ::                                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3431   \textcolor{comment}{/*      If this bit is set, only bitmaps contained in the font may be    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3432   \textcolor{comment}{/*      embedded; no outline data may be embedded.  If there are no      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3433   \textcolor{comment}{/*      bitmaps available in the font, then the font is unembeddable.    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3434   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3435   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3436   \textcolor{comment}{/*    While the fsType flags can indicate that a font may be embedded, a */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3437   \textcolor{comment}{/*    license with the font vendor may be separately required to use the */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3438   \textcolor{comment}{/*    font in this way.                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3439   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3440 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_FSTYPE\_INSTALLABLE\_EMBEDDING         0x0000}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3441 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_FSTYPE\_RESTRICTED\_LICENSE\_EMBEDDING  0x0002}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3442 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_FSTYPE\_PREVIEW\_AND\_PRINT\_EMBEDDING   0x0004}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3443 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_FSTYPE\_EDITABLE\_EMBEDDING            0x0008}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3444 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_FSTYPE\_NO\_SUBSETTING                 0x0100}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3445 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FT\_FSTYPE\_BITMAP\_EMBEDDING\_ONLY         0x0200}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3446 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3447 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3448 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3474 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3475   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3476   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Section>                                                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3477   \textcolor{comment}{/*    glyph\_variants                                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3478   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3479   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Title>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3480   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Glyph Variants                                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3481   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3482   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Abstract>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3483   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The FreeType\string~2 interface to Unicode Ideographic Variation          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3484   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Sequences (IVS), using the SFNT cmap format\string~14.                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3485   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3486   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3487   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Many CJK characters have variant forms.  They are a sort of grey   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3488   \textcolor{comment}{/*    area somewhere between being totally irrelevant and semantically   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3489   \textcolor{comment}{/*    distinct; for this reason, the Unicode consortium decided to       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3490   \textcolor{comment}{/*    introduce Ideographic Variation Sequences (IVS), consisting of a   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3491   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Unicode base character and one of 240 variant selectors            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3492   \textcolor{comment}{/*    (U+E0100-\/U+E01EF), instead of further extending the already huge   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3493   \textcolor{comment}{/*    code range for CJK characters.                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3494   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3495   \textcolor{comment}{/*    An IVS is registered and unique; for further details please refer  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3496   \textcolor{comment}{/*    to Unicode Technical Standard \#37, the Ideographic Variation       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3497   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Database:                                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3498   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3499   \textcolor{comment}{/*      http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr37/                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3500   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3501   \textcolor{comment}{/*    To date (November 2014), the character with the most variants is   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3502   \textcolor{comment}{/*    U+9089, having 32 such IVS.                                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3503   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3504   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Adobe and MS decided to support IVS with a new cmap subtable       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3505   \textcolor{comment}{/*    (format\string~14).  It is an odd subtable because it is not a mapping of */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3506   \textcolor{comment}{/*    input code points to glyphs, but contains lists of all variants    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3507   \textcolor{comment}{/*    supported by the font.                                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3508   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3509   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A variant may be either `default' or `non-\/default'.  A default     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3510   \textcolor{comment}{/*    variant is the one you will get for that code point if you look it */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3511   \textcolor{comment}{/*    up in the standard Unicode cmap.  A non-\/default variant is a       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3512   \textcolor{comment}{/*    different glyph.                                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3513   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3514 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3515 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3516 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3517 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3520   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Face\_GetCharVariantIndex                                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3521   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3522   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3523   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Return the glyph index of a given character code as modified by    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3524   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the variation selector.                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3525   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3526   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3527   \textcolor{comment}{/*    face ::                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3528   \textcolor{comment}{/*      A handle to the source face object.                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3529   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3530   \textcolor{comment}{/*    charcode ::                                                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3531   \textcolor{comment}{/*      The character code point in Unicode.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3532   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3533   \textcolor{comment}{/*    variantSelector ::                                                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3534   \textcolor{comment}{/*      The Unicode code point of the variation selector.                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3535   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3536   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3537   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The glyph index.  0\string~means either `undefined character code', or    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3538   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `undefined selector code', or `no variation selector cmap          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3539   \textcolor{comment}{/*    subtable', or `current CharMap is not Unicode'.                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3540   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3541   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3542   \textcolor{comment}{/*    If you use FreeType to manipulate the contents of font files       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3543   \textcolor{comment}{/*    directly, be aware that the glyph index returned by this function  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3544   \textcolor{comment}{/*    doesn't always correspond to the internal indices used within      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3545   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the file.  This is done to ensure that value\string~0 always corresponds  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3546   \textcolor{comment}{/*    to the `missing glyph'.                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3547   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3548   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This function is only meaningful if                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3549   \textcolor{comment}{/*      a) the font has a variation selector cmap sub table,             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3550   \textcolor{comment}{/*    and                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3551   \textcolor{comment}{/*      b) the current charmap has a Unicode encoding.                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3552   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3553   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Since>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3554   \textcolor{comment}{/*    2.3.6                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3555   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3556   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_UInt )}
\DoxyCodeLine{3557   FT\_Face\_GetCharVariantIndex( \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}   face,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3558                                FT\_ULong  charcode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3559                                FT\_ULong  variantSelector );}

\DoxyCodeLine{3696   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3697   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Section>                                                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3698   \textcolor{comment}{/*    computations                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3699   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3700   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Title>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3701   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Computations                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3702   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3703   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Abstract>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3704   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Crunching fixed numbers and vectors.                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3705   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3706   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3707   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This section contains various functions used to perform            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3708   \textcolor{comment}{/*    computations on 16.16 fixed-\/float numbers or 2d vectors.           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3709   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3710   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Order>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3711   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_MulDiv                                                          */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3720   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
