\DoxyCodeLine{3723 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3724 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3725   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3726   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3727   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_MulDiv                                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3728   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3729   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3730   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A very simple function used to perform the computation `(a*b)/c'   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3731   \textcolor{comment}{/*    with maximum accuracy (it uses a 64-\/bit intermediate integer       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3732   \textcolor{comment}{/*    whenever necessary).                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3733   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3734   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This function isn't necessarily as fast as some processor specific */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3735   \textcolor{comment}{/*    operations, but is at least completely portable.                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3736   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3737   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3738   \textcolor{comment}{/*    a :: The first multiplier.                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3739   \textcolor{comment}{/*    b :: The second multiplier.                                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3740   \textcolor{comment}{/*    c :: The divisor.                                                  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3741   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3742   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3743   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The result of `(a*b)/c'.  This function never traps when trying to */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3744   \textcolor{comment}{/*    divide by zero; it simply returns `MaxInt' or `MinInt' depending   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3745   \textcolor{comment}{/*    on the signs of `a' and `b'.                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3746   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3747   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_Long )}
\DoxyCodeLine{3748   FT\_MulDiv( FT\_Long  a,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3749              FT\_Long  b,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3750              FT\_Long  c );}
\DoxyCodeLine{3751 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3752 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3753 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3754   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3755   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3756   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_MulFix                                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3757   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3758   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3759   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A very simple function used to perform the computation             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3760   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `(a*b)/0x10000' with maximum accuracy.  Most of the time this is   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3761   \textcolor{comment}{/*    used to multiply a given value by a 16.16 fixed-\/point factor.      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3762   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3763   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3764   \textcolor{comment}{/*    a :: The first multiplier.                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3765   \textcolor{comment}{/*    b :: The second multiplier.  Use a 16.16 factor here whenever      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3766   \textcolor{comment}{/*         possible (see note below).                                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3767   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3768   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3769   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The result of `(a*b)/0x10000'.                                     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3770   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3771   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3772   \textcolor{comment}{/*    This function has been optimized for the case where the absolute   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3773   \textcolor{comment}{/*    value of `a' is less than 2048, and `b' is a 16.16 scaling factor. */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3774   \textcolor{comment}{/*    As this happens mainly when scaling from notional units to         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3775   \textcolor{comment}{/*    fractional pixels in FreeType, it resulted in noticeable speed     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3776   \textcolor{comment}{/*    improvements between versions 2.x and 1.x.                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3777   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3778   \textcolor{comment}{/*    As a conclusion, always try to place a 16.16 factor as the         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3779   \textcolor{comment}{/*    \_second\_ argument of this function; this can make a great          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3780   \textcolor{comment}{/*    difference.                                                        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3781   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3782   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_Long )}
\DoxyCodeLine{3783   FT\_MulFix( FT\_Long  a,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3784              FT\_Long  b );}
\DoxyCodeLine{3785 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3786 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3787 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3788   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3789   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3790   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_DivFix                                                          */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3791   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3792   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3793   \textcolor{comment}{/*    A very simple function used to perform the computation             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3794   \textcolor{comment}{/*    `(a*0x10000)/b' with maximum accuracy.  Most of the time, this is  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3795   \textcolor{comment}{/*    used to divide a given value by a 16.16 fixed-\/point factor.        */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3796   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3797   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3798   \textcolor{comment}{/*    a :: The numerator.                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3799   \textcolor{comment}{/*    b :: The denominator.  Use a 16.16 factor here.                    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3800   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3801   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3899   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Note that those functions and macros are of limited use because    */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3919 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3920 \textcolor{comment}{   * @enum:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3921 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FREETYPE\_XXX}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3922 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3923 \textcolor{comment}{   * @description:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3924 \textcolor{comment}{   *   These three macros identify the FreeType source code version.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3925 \textcolor{comment}{   *   Use @FT\_Library\_Version to access them at runtime.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3926 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3927 \textcolor{comment}{   * @values:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3928 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FREETYPE\_MAJOR :: The major version number.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3929 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FREETYPE\_MINOR :: The minor version number.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3930 \textcolor{comment}{   *   FREETYPE\_PATCH :: The patch level.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3931 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3932 \textcolor{comment}{   * @note:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3933 \textcolor{comment}{   *   The version number of FreeType if built as a dynamic link library}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3934 \textcolor{comment}{   *   with the `libtool' package is \_not\_ controlled by these three}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3935 \textcolor{comment}{   *   macros.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3936 \textcolor{comment}{   *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3937 \textcolor{comment}{   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3938 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FREETYPE\_MAJOR  2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3939 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FREETYPE\_MINOR  5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3940 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define FREETYPE\_PATCH  5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3941 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3942 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3943 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3944   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3945   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3946   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Library\_Version                                                 */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3947   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3948   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3949   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Return the version of the FreeType library being used.  This is    */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3950   \textcolor{comment}{/*    useful when dynamically linking to the library, since one cannot   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3951   \textcolor{comment}{/*    use the macros @FREETYPE\_MAJOR, @FREETYPE\_MINOR, and               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3952   \textcolor{comment}{/*    @FREETYPE\_PATCH.                                                   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3953   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3954   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3955   \textcolor{comment}{/*    library :: A source library handle.                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3956   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3957   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Output>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3958   \textcolor{comment}{/*    amajor  :: The major version number.                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3959   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3960   \textcolor{comment}{/*    aminor  :: The minor version number.                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3961   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3962   \textcolor{comment}{/*    apatch  :: The patch version number.                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3963   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3964   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3965   \textcolor{comment}{/*    The reason why this function takes a `library' argument is because */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3966   \textcolor{comment}{/*    certain programs implement library initialization in a custom way  */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3967   \textcolor{comment}{/*    that doesn't use @FT\_Init\_FreeType.                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3968   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3969   \textcolor{comment}{/*    In such cases, the library version might not be available before   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3970   \textcolor{comment}{/*    the library object has been created.                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3971   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3972   FT\_EXPORT( \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} )}
\DoxyCodeLine{3973   FT\_Library\_Version( FT\_Library   library,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3974                       FT\_Int      *amajor,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3975                       FT\_Int      *aminor,}
\DoxyCodeLine{3976                       FT\_Int      *apatch );}
\DoxyCodeLine{3977 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3979 \textcolor{comment}{  /*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3980   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3981   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Function>                                                            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3982   \textcolor{comment}{/*    FT\_Face\_CheckTrueTypePatents                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3983   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3984   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Description>                                                         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3985   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Parse all bytecode instructions of a TrueType font file to check   */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3986   \textcolor{comment}{/*    whether any of the patented opcodes are used.  This is only useful */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3987   \textcolor{comment}{/*    if you want to be able to use the unpatented hinter with           */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3988   \textcolor{comment}{/*    fonts that do *not* use these opcodes.                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3989   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3990   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Note that this function parses *all* glyph instructions in the     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3991   \textcolor{comment}{/*    font file, which may be slow.                                      */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3992   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3993   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Input>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3994   \textcolor{comment}{/*    face :: A face handle.                                             */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3995   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3996   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Return>                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3997   \textcolor{comment}{/*    1\string~if this is a TrueType font that uses one of the patented         */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3998   \textcolor{comment}{/*    opcodes, 0\string~otherwise.                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3999   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4000   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Note>                                                                */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4001   \textcolor{comment}{/*    Since May 2010, TrueType hinting is no longer patented.            */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4002   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4003   \textcolor{comment}{/* <Since>                                                               */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4004   \textcolor{comment}{/*    2.3.5                                                              */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4005   \textcolor{comment}{/*                                                                       */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4006   FT\_EXPORT( FT\_Bool )}
\DoxyCodeLine{4007   FT\_Face\_CheckTrueTypePatents( \mbox{\hyperlink{structFT__FaceRec__}{FT\_Face}}  face );}
\DoxyCodeLine{4008 }
